Now is the hottest period in summer. The quilt is probably used in winter. It is super thick. Also hot without a quilt!
Service: The front desk staff are not enthusiastic, they speak bluntly and have no expression
The most eye-catching feature of the hotel is the swimming pool, which should be the first in Xiangyang. Those who like swimming can recommend it!
